# Analysis

## Ground Truth (GT)

The GT expression is:
$$f(t, A) = 0.2084703204063362 \cdot A^{0.333333} - 0.6750544468008356 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.0783132263146032 \cdot t}$$

This has two terms:
1. A term proportional to $A^{1/3}$ (cube root of A)
2. A term proportional to $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ where $\alpha \approx 0.0783$

The key basis functions are: $A^{1/3}$ and $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$.

## Candidate Analysis

Let me check each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Critical observation:** The GT requires $A^{1/3}$ (a fractional power of A). None of the candidates contain $A^{c}$ with a free exponent except **Candidate 47**.

Most candidates use combinations of:
- $A/(c_1 + t)$ вҖ” linear in A, rational in t
- $\exp(A \cdot c)$ вҖ” exponential in A
- $\log(A \cdot c + 1)$ вҖ” logarithmic in A
- $\exp(c \cdot t)$ вҖ” exponential in t
- $t/(c + t)$ вҖ” rational in t
- $\sin$, $\tanh$ вҖ” trigonometric/hyperbolic

**None of these basis functions can produce $A^{1/3}$.**

Let me check **Candidate 47** specifically:
$$c_1 \cdot A^{c_0} + c_2 \cdot \sin(c_3 t + c_4) + c_5 \cdot t \cdot (A + c_6)^{c_7} + \tanh(c_8 t + c_9)$$

This has $A^{c_0}$ which can match $A^{1/3}$ by setting $c_0 = 1/3$.

For the second GT term $-0.675 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.0783t}$, we need $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$. Candidate 47 has:
- $c_5 \cdot t \cdot (A + c_6)^{c_7}$ вҖ” this has a factor of $t$ and a power of $(A + c_6)$
- $c_2 \cdot \sin(c_3 t + c_4)$ вҖ” sinusoidal, not exponential decay
- $\tanh(c_8 t + c_9)$ вҖ” hyperbolic tangent, not $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$

None of these can produce $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$. Even setting $c_5 = 0$ to eliminate the $t(A+c_6)^{c_7}$ term, we'd be left with $A^{c_0} c_1 + \sin(\cdot) + \tanh(\cdot)$, which cannot match $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$.

**For all other candidates (1-46, 48-50):** They use $\log(A \cdot c + 1)$ as the A-dependent non-linear term. While $\log(Ac + 1)$ can approximate $A^{1/3}$ numerically over some range, it is NOT mathematically equivalent to $A^{1/3}$ for all A. These are linearly independent functions. Similarly, $\exp(A \cdot c)$ is not equivalent to $A^{1/3}$.

For the time-dependent part, many candidates use $\exp(c \cdot t)$ which could match $e^{-\alpha t}$, and $A/(c+t)$ which is rational in $t$ rather than exponential. The product $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ requires both $A$ and $e^{-\alpha t}$ multiplied together. In candidates with $\exp(A \cdot c_4)$, the exponential depends on $A$, not just $t$.

Candidates 3-6, 15-17, 20, 31-40, 45 use $\exp(c \cdot t)$ (exponential in $t$ only), but they don't have $A \cdot \exp(c \cdot t)$ вҖ” the $A$ dependence comes through $\log(A \cdot c + 1)$, not through multiplication with the exponential.

**No candidate has both $A^{1/3}$ and $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ as achievable basis functions.**

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK17)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_f*A**c3
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze whether any candidate can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT:** `0.2084703204063362*A**0.333333333333333 - 0.6750544468008356*A*exp(-0.0783132263146032*t)`

The GT has two terms:
1. A term proportional to `A^(1/3)` (constant in t)
2. A term proportional to `A * exp(-Оұt)` where Оұ вүҲ 0.0783

Key observations about the GT's functional form:
- It depends on A through `A^(1/3)` and `A*exp(-Оұt)`
- The A^(1/3) term has no t-dependence
- The exponential decay is in t only (not in A)

Now let me examine the candidates. Most candidates use basis functions like:
- `A/(c+t)`, `1/(c+t)`, `exp(A*c)/(c+t)`, `log(A*c+1)/(c+t)`, `t*exp(A*c)/(c+t)`, `t*log(A*c+1)/(c+t)`, `t/(c+t)`
- Or: `exp(c*t)/(c+t)`, `t*exp(c*t)/(c+t)`, `log(A*c+1)/(c+t)`, `t*log(A*c+1)/(c+t)`

**Critical structural analysis:**

The GT contains `A*exp(-Оұt)` вҖ” this is a product of A and an exponential in t. None of the candidates in the "exp(c*t)" family (Candidates 3-6, 15-17, 20, 31-40, etc.) have a term that couples A with exp(t). They have `exp(c*t)` terms (no A dependence in the exponential's coefficient of t) and separate `log(A*c+1)` terms.

The GT also contains `A^(1/3)`. No candidate has a power-law `A^c` term. Some use `log(A*c+1)` which is NOT equivalent to `A^(1/3)` вҖ” these are linearly independent functions.

**Candidates with `exp(A*c)` terms** (1, 2, 7-14, 18-19, 21-30, 42-43): These have `exp(A*c4)` which is exponential IN A, not `A*exp(c*t)`. The GT needs `A*exp(c*t)`, which is fundamentally different from `exp(c*A)`.

**Candidate 47:** `A**c0*c1 + c2*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*t*(A + c6)**c7 + tanh(c8*t + c9)`
This has `A^c0` which could match `A^(1/3)`. But for the second term, it needs `A*exp(-Оұt)`. It has `sin`, `tanh`, and `t*(A+c6)^c7`. None of these can produce `A*exp(-Оұt)`. `sin` and `tanh` are not exponential decay functions. **NO MATCH.**

**Candidate 41:** `A*c0/(c1*t + c2) + c3*t/(c4 + t) + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*t + c8/(c1*t + c2) + c9`
This has `A/(c1*t+c2)` (rational in t, not exponential), `exp(c6*t)` (no A coupling), and no `A^(1/3)` term. **NO MATCH.**

**Candidate 44:** `A*c0/(c1*t + c2) + c3*t*exp(c4*t) + c5*t + c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8/(c1*t + c2) + c9`
Has `A/(c1*t+c2)` not `A*exp(ct)`, and `log(A*c+1)` not `A^(1/3)`. **NO MATCH.**

After careful analysis, **no candidate** has the correct basis functions. The GT requires:
1. `A^(1/3)` вҖ” no candidate has this (they use `log(A*c+1)` or `A` or `exp(A*c)`)
2. `A*exp(c*t)` вҖ” no candidate has this coupling of A with exponential in t

Every candidate verdict is [NO MATCH].
